--- Foglio: Tyre Temp Optimiser ---
Cella I8: =IF(J8=0,"OK",IF(J8<0,"Under","Over"))
Cella J8: =(D8-C8)-(E8-D8)
Cella L8: =IF(E8-C8=$D$5,"OK",IF(E8-C8>$D$5,"Too Much","Too Little"))
Cella M8: =(E8-C8)
Cella O8: =IF(P8>$B$5+$C$5,"Hot",IF(P8<$B$5-$C$5,"Cold","OK"))
Cella P8: =AVERAGE(C8:E8  )
Cella R8: ="Frt: " & ROUND(AVERAGE(P8,P14),1)
Cella T8: ="Left: " & CHAR(10) & ROUND(AVERAGE(P8,P10),1)
Cella V8: =AVERAGE(P8,P14)
Cella W8: =IF(V8<$B$5-$C$5,1,IF(V8>$B$5+$C$5,3,2))
Cella R9: =IF(AND(W8=2,W14=2),"Balanced",IF(AND(W8<>2,W14=2),"Understeer", IF(AND(W14<>2,W8=2),"Oversteer", IF(AND(W8=1,W14=1),"Frt & Rear Too Cold", IF(AND(W8=3,W14=3),"Frt & Rr Too Hot", IF(AND(W8=3,W14=1),"Likely Understeer", IF(AND(W8=1,W14=3),"Likely Oversteer")))))))
Cella I10: =IF(J10=0,"OK",IF(J10<0,"Under","Over"))
Cella J10: =(D10-C10)-(E10-D10)
Cella L10: =IF(E10-C10=$E$5,"OK",IF(E10-C10>$E$5,"Too Much","Too Little"))
Cella M10: =(E10-C10)
Cella O10: =IF(P10>$B$5+$C$5,"Hot",IF(P10<$B$5-$C$5,"Cold","OK"))
